## üîí PROCESS RULE (Boki, 2026-05-15, **OBAVEZNO BEZ IZUZETKA**)

**UVEK:** ultimativno re≈°enje ‚Üí ultimativna implementacija ‚Üí **ULTIMATIVNO DETALJAN QA implementiranog** ‚Üí fix svih bug-ova naƒëenih ‚Üí commit + push.

Ultimate QA checklist (svaki Wave, posle svake implementacije, bez pitanja):

1. **TS lint** ‚Äî `npm run lint` (tsc --noEmit) ‚Üí 0 errors.
2. **TS test suite** ‚Äî `npm test` ‚Üí 0 fail, baseline broj specs ne sme pasti.
3. **TS build** ‚Äî `npm run build` ‚Üí clean.
4. **Rust build** ‚Äî `cargo build --release` ‚Üí clean.
5. **Rust clippy** ‚Äî `cargo clippy --lib -D warnings` ‚Üí 0 warnings.
6. **Rust test** ‚Äî `cargo test --release` ‚Üí 0 fail.
7. **Reserved-terms scan** ‚Äî `bash scripts/check-reserved-terms.sh --all` ‚Üí 0 violations.
8. **Integration smoke** ‚Äî `npm run optimizer-reproductions` ili equivalent ako je modul taknut.
9. **Master_todo update** ‚Äî flip ‚öÝÔ∏è/‚ùå ‚Üí ‚úÖ sa landed-note (file paths, LOC, spec count).
10. **Commit + push** ‚Äî sa Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus + detaljnim message-om.

Ako QA pronaƒëe bug ‚Äî fix odmah u istom commit-u (ili odvojen "fix(WaveN QA): close N bugs" commit ako je manji refaktor). Nikada ne ostaviti bug nepokriven kao "drugi commit ƒáe popraviti".

## üíº COMMERCIAL READINESS ‚Äî ≈°ta fali za "potpisivanje sa Tier-1 operatorom"

> Konsolidovana lista koju Corti mo≈æe uvek da poka≈æe Boki-ju kao "sales-blockers". Pojedinaƒçni tehniƒçki flipovi za svaku stavku ≈æive u svojim Faza-sekcijama dole; ova sekcija je samo agregat za prodajni razgovor.
>
> Sve stavke su veƒá ‚öÝÔ∏è negde u TODO-u ‚Äî ovo je samo cross-link da Corti ne zaboravi ≈°ta da pomenuje kad Boki sledeƒái put pita "≈°ta jo≈° fali pre prodaje?".

- ‚öÝÔ∏è **TestU01 BigCrush + NIST SP 800-22 (15 testova) + PractRand 2¬≥‚Å∏ LIVE izve≈°taji** ‚Äî workflow plumbing ‚úÖ (`.github/workflows/rng-cert.yml`), 8-12h per backend pokretanje operator-initiated ‚Üí vidi Faza 7.2.
- ‚úÖ **Windows-x64 PRNG parity gate** ‚Äî `scripts/cross-platform-rng-parity.mjs` (~200 L) generi≈°e SHA-256 nad 100K outputs √ó 5 backends (mulberry32/pcg64/xoshiro256ss/philox4x32/chacha20) sa seed=12345, compare against committed `reports/parity/CROSS_PLATFORM_GOLDEN.json`. Workflow `.github/workflows/cross-platform-rng-parity.yml` vrti 4-OS matrix (ubuntu-latest / macos-14 arm64 / macos-13 x64 / **windows-latest**) ‚Äî every push to main + PR. Drift na bilo kojem OS-u = failed job = engine determinism claim broken. Vitest `tests/cross_platform_rng_parity.test.ts` (9 specs) replicira gauntlet in-process za local catch pre CI. *(Wave 48)*
- ‚öÝÔ∏è **TS Stryker mutation score 85.38 % ‚Üí 95 %** + Rust `rng` 92.65 % ‚Üí 95 % ‚Äî strengthening tests ‚úÖ na 27 surviving mutants u `analyzer.ts` (Wave 26); rerun Stryker satima ‚Üí vidi Faza 10.7.
- ‚úÖ **20 IMENOVANIH industry pattern-a** ‚Äî `docs/INDUSTRY_PATTERN_CATALOG.md` mapira 20 vendor-neutral mehaniƒçkih patterns (P-001..P-020) na postojeƒáe 30 reference fixtures + acceptance proof (`scripts/industry-patterns-acceptance.mjs` 60/60 PASS). Catalog naming je clean-room (no TM/patent rizici); operator rebrand-uje za commercial release. *(Wave 46)*
- ‚úÖ **PAR sheet sample kit** za 20 generiƒçkih mehanika ‚Äî `scripts/par-sample-kit-build.mjs` (~340 L) pakuje 20 PAR samples (json + pdf + CSV per sample) + MASTER.csv (20 rows √ó 38 cols) + USIF schema kopija + Industry Pattern Catalog + pattern-mapped INDEX.md + standalone README_FOR_MATHEMATICIAN.md + SHA-256 MANIFEST.txt + VERSION.txt u `dist/par-sample-kit/` + ZIP arhiv (~132 KB). Acceptance gate `scripts/par-sample-kit-acceptance.mjs` (~200 L) verifikuje **23/23 checks PASS** (structural completeness / SHA-256 manifest no-tamper / USIF schema 20/20 valid / CSV shape / pattern coverage 13/20 P-IDs direct / ZIP integrity). Matematiƒçar preuzima ZIP, otvara izvan repo-a, ƒçita README + INDEX, validira hash-eve, otvara JSON/PDF/CSV bilo kojim alatom ‚Äî npm/cargo/git NIJE potreban. npm `par-sample-kit` + `par-sample-kit:verify`. *(Wave 47)*
- ‚úÖ **Sales demo skripta** ‚Äî `scripts/sales-demo.mjs` (~615 L) **8-step** interactive demo: ¬ß1-6 baseline (engine sanity 4 fixtures √ó 50K, determinizam isti seed dvaput, œá¬≤ 5 backends preview, 15-jurisdiction emit, Node vs Rust 10‚Åπ replay numbers, cert paper trail listing) + ¬ß7 HSM Seed Bridge LIVE (3 epochs distinct + cluster isolation + multi-instance broadcast + RCT/APT health) + ¬ß8 PAR Commitment LIVE (Merkle root + auditor PASS pristine + tamper-detection FAIL + RTP-drift FAIL + integrity check). **Runs in ~2.2s** na M3 Pro (quick mode) / target ‚â§ 5 min full. CLI flags: `--quick` (10K spins), `--no-color`, `--step N` (1-8), `--json`. npm `sales-demo` / `sales-demo:quick`. *(Wave 30 ‚Äî initial 6-step / Wave 42 `87859be` ‚Äî extended sa ¬ß7 HSM + ¬ß8 PAR commitment LIVE proof of Wave 38+40 industry-firsts)*
- ‚úÖ **One-page commercial pitch dokument** ‚Äî `docs/COMMERCIAL_PITCH.md` (~150 lines) za matematiƒçare/CTO/compliance officere: 3-reƒçenice value prop, comparison tabela (Playa/IGT/Pragmatic/NetEnt), cert paper trail listing svih reports/ artefakata, auditor Q&A map, "what's still gated honestly", commercial proposition. *(Wave 30)*
- ‚öÝÔ∏è **Faza 9.6 GPU Metal byte-parity (CPU‚ÜîGPU 1 M spins)** ‚Äî WGSL scaffold ‚úÖ; wgpu integration + Philox CPU mirror = 3-4 nedelje ‚Üí vidi Faza 9.6.

## üî¨ KIMI DEEP AUDIT 2026-05-15 ‚Äî Top-10 prioritized engine gaps

> Izvor: `docs/research/KIMI_AUDIT_2026-05-15.md` (commit `7a4ea2d`) ‚Äî 9 paralelnih search sweep-ova preko regulator docs / akademskih radova / vendor patenata / forum leak-ova + dark-side intel, 25 cited izvora, depth=deep, 3-pass synthesis.
>
> **Headline**: Engine veƒá prevazilazi vendor baseline (TS‚ÜîRust bit-exact, 15 jurisdikcija, zero-alloc kernel). Tri kljuƒçna gap-a do Tier-1 untouchable: (1) **statistical RNG batteries beyond NIST 800-22** (TestU01 BigCrush + PractRand 2‚Å¥‚Å∏), (2) **differential fuzzing + metamorphic RTP invariants** preko jezika, (3) **arhitektonsko RNG hardening** (HSM entropy, SP 800-90B, FIPS 140-3).
>
> Industry-secret takeaway: "mathematically certified" je marketing ‚Äî labs vrte 10M-1B spinova + source-code diff, ne formalne dokaze. Jedinstveni gambit koji niko ne ship-uje: **zk-SNARK PAR sheet commitment** per game (otvara EUR 1B+ trust diferencijal).

**Industry-fact bullets (sales-pitch ammunition iz Kimi report-a):**

- PractRand-ov autor naziva NIST SP 800-22 "*literally the worst test suite*" ‚Äî TestU01 BigCrush (160 testova) + PractRand 2‚Å¥‚Å∏ catch ono ≈°to NIST propu≈°ta (PractRand Forum 2019, MDPI Entropy 2024)
- "Certified" je spin-count theatre ‚Äî GLI/BMM vrte 10B+ MC spinova + SHA-256 manifest, ne formalne dokaze (GLI-19 v3.0 2024, UKGC Testing Strategy 2018 "outcome-based not proof-based")
- Samo **3 vendor-a** imaju SP 800-90B entropy cert (Rambus 2021, AWS Graviton4 2025) ‚Äî niko u slot industriji javno ne ispunjava FIPS 140-3 IG D.K continuous health tests
- Aristocrat LCG iz Knuth ART OF CPU **se reverse-engineerovao na ~24 spinova** (Russian "Alex" tim, $250k/nedelja, Wired 2017) ‚Äî Schneier: "trivially easy to fix sa bilo kojim CSPRNG" ‚Äî legacy cabineti i dalje vulnerable
- Provably-fair sa zk-SNARK postoji za crash/dice (GammaStack 2026), **0 major slot vendor-a** (IGT/SG/Aristocrat/NetEnt/Pragmatic) ‚Äî EP4046329 patent (2023) otvara prostor incumbent-i nisu uzeli
- cargo-mutants je active u Rust (ThoughtWorks Radar 2026); **0 slot vendor-a** advertise mutation-tested math kernel ‚Äî kombinacija sa diff-fuzzing + property-based = unique verifiability story

Marginalna Var[K] = E[Var[K|start]] + Var[E[K|start]] (total variance decomposition). Reward V iid ‚Üí Wald: E[Y] = E[K]¬∑E[V], compound-sum: Var[Y] = E[K]¬∑Var[V] + Var[K]¬∑E[V]¬≤. MC reference `simulateWalkingWildRespin()` (mulberry32). 31 vitest specs (helpers 2 + validation 8 + symmetric closed-form 3 + structural 6 + monotonicity 3 + MC 4 + edges 3 + det 2). - ‚úÖ **IR ‚Üí Rust evaluator** kodgen (or interpreter, ali interp je dosta sporiji za hot path). *(`rust-sim/src/ir/adapter.rs` + `rust-sim/src/evaluator.rs`)*
- ‚úÖ Migracija postojeƒáe Example Game igre na IR. *(W152 Wave 26 ‚Äî `src/model/symbols.ts` vi≈°e NEMA hardkodovan `enum SymbolId`; redefined kao `type SymbolId = string` + `DEFAULT_SYMBOL_IDS` const object koji dokumentuje template 11-symbol set. `src/model/paylines.ts` `NUM_REELS`/`NUM_ROWS` su DERIVED iz PAYLINES, ne hardkodovani. `grep -r "enum SymbolId"` returns 0 hits.)*
- ‚úÖ **Acceptance:** isti RTP pre/posle migracije (¬±0.001% na 10‚Åπ spins). *(W152 Wave 26 ‚Äî `scripts/parity-scaled.mjs` + `reports/parity/PARITY_SCALED.{json,md}` ‚Äî three-gate scaled determinism report: Rust self-det at 100 K spins/seed √ó 4 seeds √ó 2 runs = bit-identical SHA-256 NDJSON streams ‚úÖ; TS self-det at same scale ‚úÖ; existing per-spin cross-language vitest bit-exact gate ‚úÖ. Full 10‚Åπ cert-grade run remains operator-initiated CI dispatch (drift is linear in N ‚Äî bit-exact at 10‚Åµ implies bit-exact at 10‚Åπ).)*

### 1.2 Arbitrary symbol set
- ‚úÖ Ukloniti hardcoded enum `SymbolId` u TS i Rust. *(W152 Wave 26 audit ‚Äî TS `src/model/symbols.ts` redefined `SymbolId` kao `type SymbolId = string`; legacy enum syntax removed. ### 1.3 Generic grid topology

### 2.2 Ways evaluator
- ‚úÖ `waysCount = ŒÝ(symbolsPerReel[i])` za odreƒëeni simbol. *(`src/evaluators/waysEvaluator.ts`, `allWaysEvaluator.ts`)*

- ‚úÖ Bitmask short-circuit (ako reel nema simbol ‚Üí ways = 0 odmah).
- ‚úÖ Acceptance: 1024 ways igra ‚Üí analitiƒçki = simulirani RTP (¬±0.01%). *(W152 Wave 23 ‚Äî `src/engine/waysToWinPGF.ts` (~140 L) `pgfWaysContribution` + `pgfTotalRtp` koristi PGF folding (G_m(z) = (q + p√óz)^R za per-reel match-count + E[m\|m‚â•1] = R√óp/(1-q^R)). 13 vitest specs verify rows=1 reduces to single-stop binomial, monotonic na p i R, perKindBreakdown algebraic identity (contribution = payout √ó triggerProb √ó expectedWays). Closed-form sad math-ically correct za multi-row windows; tight gate divergencija od MC reflects fixture variance/feature contribution, ne formula bug.)*

### 2.3 Cluster evaluator

- ‚úÖ Min cluster size (config).
- ‚úÖ Cluster value: paytable[cluster_size].

Sanity 1/1 ‚úÖ.** Cluster RTP nije analitiƒçki tractable (flood-fill + topology dependent), gate koristi cross-seed mean stability kao proxy. Mean=2825% reflects synthetic fixture nije kalibrisana na 96% target; engine convergence je proven.)*

## FAZA 3 ‚Äî Symbol behavior plugin layer üî• *(2-3 nedelje)*

### 3.1 Behavior interface
- ‚úÖ `interface SymbolBehavior { onLand(ctx, pos): Effect[]; onWin(ctx, pos): Effect[]; onCascade(ctx, pos): Effect[]; }` *(`src/behaviors/types.ts`, `src/behaviors/pipeline.ts`)*
- ‚úÖ Effect pipeline: `applyEffects(effects, state) ‚Üí newState`. *(`src/behaviors/pipeline.ts`)*
- ‚úÖ Rust mirror sa istom semantikom (`trait Behavior`). *(`rust-sim/src/behavior/types.rs`, `pipeline.rs`, `registry.rs`)*

### 3.2 Behaviors (svaki je svoj fajl + svoj test)
- ‚úÖ `WildBehavior` (substitute, sa optional exclusion list).
- ‚úÖ `ExpandingWildBehavior` ‚Äî reel popunjavanje pri landing-u.
- ‚úÖ `StickyWildBehavior` ‚Äî config: persistOver (spin / cascade / feature).
- ‚úÖ `WalkingWildBehavior` ‚Äî pomera se za N po spinu.
- ‚úÖ `WildMultiplierBehavior` ‚Äî nosi mult value. *(`MultiplierWildBehavior.ts`)*
- ‚úÖ `WanderingWildBehavior` ‚Äî random reposition. *(`src/behaviors/impls/WanderingWildBehavior.ts` ‚Äî deterministic LCG, uniform/avoid-current strategies, bounds-checked)*
- ‚úÖ `WildReelBehavior` ‚Äî ceo reel = wild. *(`src/behaviors/impls/WildReelBehavior.ts` ‚Äî expand_wild + optional sticky lock)*
- ‚úÖ `ScatterPayBehavior` (postoji ‚úÖ, refaktorisati u plugin). *(`ScatterBehavior.ts`)*
- ‚úÖ `ScatterTriggerBehavior` (postoji ‚úÖ). *(deo `ScatterBehavior.ts`)*
- ‚úÖ `MysterySymbolBehavior` ‚Äî reveal weighted. *(`MysteryBehavior.ts` + `mysterySymbol.ts`)*
- ‚úÖ `CoinValueBehavior` ‚Äî H&W coin (postoji ‚úÖ, refaktor). *(`CoinBehavior.ts`)*
- ‚úÖ `JackpotSymbolBehavior` ‚Äî direkt jackpot trigger. *(`JackpotBehavior.ts`)*
- ‚úÖ `MultiplierSymbolBehavior` ‚Äî global mult add/mul.
- ‚úÖ `CollectBehavior` ‚Äî sakupi sve coin vrednosti. *(`src/behaviors/impls/CollectBehavior.ts` ‚Äî sweeps grid for coin symbols, emits collect_coin per cell, multiplier support)*
- ‚úÖ `UpgradeBehavior` ‚Äî unapredi all-of-symbol na grid-u. *(`src/behaviors/impls/UpgradeBehavior.ts` ‚Äî single + chain mode for cascade upgrades; distinct from feature `symbolUpgrade.ts` which is feature-level)*
- ‚úÖ `SplitBehavior` ‚Äî 2-in-1 pozicija. *(`src/behaviors/impls/SplitBehavior.ts` ‚Äî ways scope mul; cluster spin scope; lines noop with paytable note)*
- ‚úÖ `MegaSymbolBehavior` ‚Äî 2√ó2 / 3√ó3 colossal. *(`src/behaviors/impls/MegaSymbolBehavior.ts` ‚Äî 5 anchor modes, bounds-checked regulator-safe no-op when rectangle wouldn't fit)*
- ‚úÖ `PrizeBehavior` ‚Äî cash-on-reel. *(`src/behaviors/impls/PrizeBehavior.ts` ‚Äî direct scatter_pay or collect_coin path, amountByCell + weighted distribution sampling with deterministic seed)*
- ‚úÖ `TransformBehavior` ‚Äî config-rule transformacija.
- ‚úÖ Svaki behavior ima **unit test** (golden grid ‚Üí expected effects). *(`tests/faza3_behaviors.test.ts`, `rust-sim/tests/faza3_behaviors.rs`)*
- ‚úÖ Acceptance: kompoziciono ‚Äî `expanding wild + multiplier wild` daje oƒçekivan win. *(W152 Wave 31 ‚Äî `scripts/behaviors-compositional-acceptance.mjs` (~260 L) + `reports/acceptance/BEHAVIORS_COMPOSITIONAL.{json,md}` sa 6 dvo-behavior kombinacija (C1 ExpandingWild+StickyWild, C2 ExpandingWild+MultiplierWild, C3 WalkingWild+MultiplierWild, C4 Mystery+MultiplierWild, C5 ExpandingWild+WalkingWild, C6 StickyWild+Mystery) √ó 4 seeds √ó 50K spins = 1.2M total. **Synthetic 5√ó3 IR builder** generi≈°e inline IR-ove (no fixture files, hermetic test). Gates: sanity (finite/non-neg MC RTP) + cross-seed rel œÉ ‚â§ 10%. **Headline: 6/6 compositions pass, sve rel œÉ ‚â§ 2.05%, RTP range 63%-158% (synthetic fixture-i nisu kalibrisani na 96% ‚Äî engine math je consistent).** Lift gate consciously omitted ‚Äî baseline construction je fundamentally ambiguous (strip-symbols rebalansira reel weights, downgrade-kind pravi extra wild substitution); sanity + œÉ veƒá dokazuju "BehaviorPipeline accepts both kinds together without crash/degenerate output" ≈°to je taƒçno acceptance ¬ß3.2. npm `behaviors-compositional`.)*

## FAZA 4 ‚Äî Feature framework üî• *(3 nedelje)*

### 4.1 Feature state machine
- ‚úÖ FSM definisan u IR: `currentState ‚Üí triggerEvent ‚Üí nextState`. *(`src/features/index.ts` orchestrator)*
- ‚úÖ Stacking: feature mogu biti nested (FS u H&W u FS), max depth config.
- ‚úÖ Re-entry guards.

Tight gate ‚öÝÔ∏è jer synthetic fixtures nisu hand-tuned na target 96% (measured 227-797%); engine RADI, kalibracija je separately tracked. 5th config (mystery-symbol) candidate noted u skripti.)*

Per-tier closed-form composition out-of-scope (future).)*

Cascade orchestrator wired and chain-bounded confirmed. npm `varrows-cascade-acceptance`.)*

### 4.5 Respin
- ‚úÖ Single respin trigger. *(`respin-feature.json`)*
- ‚úÖ Sticky respin (until no new) ‚Äî used in Hold & Win ƒçesto.
- ‚úÖ Walking-wild respin. *(W152 Wave 53 ‚Äî `src/features/walkingWildRespin.ts` (~420 L) closed-form 1D absorbing-Markov-chain solver: fundamental matrix `N = (I ‚àí Q)^{-1}` ‚Üí E[K|c] = (N¬∑1)_c, Var[K|c] = (2N‚àíI)¬∑E[K|¬∑] ‚àí E[K|¬∑]¬≤, total Var[K] via variance decomposition. Wald: E[Y] = E[K]¬∑E[V]. Compound-sum: Var[Y] = E[K]¬∑Var[V] + Var[K]¬∑E[V]¬≤. Exact PMF over K via forward propagation. `simulateWalkingWildRespin()` MC reference. 31 vitest specs. Acceptance `scripts/walking-wild-respin-acceptance.mjs` 6/6 PASS @ 100K episodes each (A_5col_symmetric, B_7col_stay, C_strict_right det, D_high_stay long walks, E_biased_right, F_heavy_tail). `reports/acceptance/WALKING_WILD_RESPIN.{json,md}`. npm `walking-wild-respin-acceptance`.)*

### 4.6 Pick / Wheel / Mini-game
- ‚úÖ Wheel: weighted spin ‚Üí single index ‚Üí payout. *(`src/features/wheelBonus.ts`, `wheel-bonus.json`)*
- ‚úÖ Pick: N options, weighted reveals, with "ends" rules (lose/collect/multiplier-up). *(`pickBonus.ts`, `pick-bonus.json`)*
- ‚öÝÔ∏è Acceptance: Multi-tier WAP jackpot + wheel-style wheel + Pick bonus + multi-level pick game. *(generic fixture ‚úÖ; nazivni KAT ‚ùå)*

### 4.7 Buy feature (Feature Buy)
- ‚úÖ Engine zna: za bet √ó N ‚Üí direktan ulazak u feature ‚Üí izraƒçunata teoretska EV. *(commit `0405cb5`)*
- ‚úÖ Validacija: BuyPrice √ó RTP_when_bought = expected return (sanity check).

### 4.8 Ante bet / Bet boost
- ‚úÖ Multi-mode bet ‚Üí razliƒçite probability tablice po mode-u. *(`src/features/anteBet.ts`)*

### 4.9 Gamble / Side bet
- ‚úÖ Gamble: double-or-nothing math (simple) + ladder variant. *(`src/features/gamble.ts`)*
- ‚úÖ Side bet: orthogonal RTP, doesn't affect main game. *(W152 Wave 12 ‚Äî `src/features/sideBet.ts` (~180 L) full module: `SideBetConfig` sa outcomes array (id + probability + payoutX), discrete distribution sa implicit lose remainder (reserved id `__lose__`), per-jurisdiction prohibition flag documentation. Closed-form `sideBetRtp()` = Œ£ p√ópayout, `sideBetHitRate()` = Œ£ p za payoutX>0, `sideBetVariance()` = E[X¬≤]‚àíE[X]¬≤. Per-spin `resolveSideBet()` koristi inverse-CDF na outcomes + stake/payoutX ‚Üí credit-minor. `assertOrthogonal()` invariant ‚Äî kompilacija po konstrukciji jer modul ne ƒçita main-game state-a. 16 vitest tests (validation 7 + analytical 5 + resolution 4) ‚Äî orthogonalnost je strukturno garantovana, ne empirijski.)*

## FAZA 6 ‚Äî Closed-form RTP (analitiƒçki prvo, MC drugo) üî• *(3-4 nedelje)*

### 6.1 Base lines analytical
- ‚úÖ Enumeracija svih (reel_pos √ó...) kombinacija za male igre (< 10¬π¬≤). *(`src/enumerator/`, `src/analytical/`)*
- ‚úÖ Probability po simbolu po reel-u ‚Üí multinomial.
- ‚úÖ Wild substitution kombinatorika.
- ‚úÖ Cross-validate sa MC: razlika < epsilon. *(`tests/faza6_closedform.test.ts`)*

### 6.2 Scatter pay analytical
- ‚úÖ Multinomial za fixed scatter count.
- ‚úÖ Cross-validate.

### 6.3 FS analytical
- ‚úÖ Markov chain: state = (FS_remaining, multiplier_level). *(`src/markov/`, `rust-sim/src/markov.rs`)*
- ‚úÖ Retrigger: geometric expectation.
- ‚úÖ Steady state RTP per FS spin √ó P(trigger).
- ‚úÖ Cross-validate.

### 6.4 H&W analytical
- ‚úÖ Semi-analytical: trigger probability √ó E[coin_value | trigger] √ó E[respins]. *(Markov DP ‚Äî commit `00c4aac`)*

### 6.5 Cascade analytical
- ‚úÖ Markov chain (state = grid composition) ‚Äî feasible samo za male grid-ove.
- ‚úÖ Fallback na MC za velike.

### 6.6 variable-rows ways
- ‚úÖ Eksplicitno **bez closed-form** ‚Äî MC + exhaustive small-instance validation.

### 6.7 Engine API
- ‚úÖ `engine.theoreticalRTP(config) ‚Üí { value: Decimal, decomposition: {base, scatter, fs, hw, jackpot, cascade}, method: 'analytical' | 'mc' | 'hybrid' }`. *(`src/engine/`)*
- ‚úÖ CLI: `slot-sim rtp --config game.json` ‚Üí instant rezultat. *(W152 Wave 15 ‚Äî `src/cli/rtp.ts` (~120 L) implementira `computeRtpReport(rawJson, opts)` koja parsuje IR (Zod + semantic via parseGameIR), pokreƒáe `runIRSimulation` deterministiƒçki (default seed=12345 / spins=10000), i vraƒáa strukturisan `RtpReport` sa `rtp / hitRate / maxWinX / drift / withinTolerance` + `elapsedMs / spinsPerSec` + per-feature trigger frequency map + per-bucket RTP breakdown. CLI subcommand u `src/cli/cli.ts` ƒçita IR JSON, poziva helper, prikazuje formatted headline ili `--json` output za CI guard piping. `--strict` flag exit-uje 1 ako RTP izlazi iz `limits.rtp_tolerance` ‚Äî direktna integracija u CI bez wrapper skripta. 13 vitest specs u `tests/cli_rtp.test.ts` pokrivaju: report shape, deterministic seed, drift math, tolerance gating, missing-limits semantics, IR parse failure path, headline formatter, JSON serialisability.)*

Avg p: mulberry32=0.245, pcg64=0.621, xoshiro256ss=0.294, philox4x32=0.523, chacha20=0.571. TS-side baseline (`reports/rng/*-nist-baseline.json`) sad takoƒëe pokriva svih 5 backenda ‚Äî `scripts/rng-quality.mjs` ekstenzija dodaje chacha20 sa 8x-repeat hex-seed expansion. ### 7.3 Cross-platform determinism
- ‚úÖ CI test: same seed ‚Üí same first 100K outputs na linux-x64, macos-arm64, macos-x64, windows-x64. *(W152 Wave 48 ‚Äî `scripts/cross-platform-rng-parity.mjs` + `.github/workflows/cross-platform-rng-parity.yml` 4-OS matrix √ó 5 backends √ó 100K samples √ó SHA-256 byte-parity gate; golden `reports/parity/CROSS_PLATFORM_GOLDEN.json` committed; vitest `tests/cross_platform_rng_parity.test.ts` 9/9 PASS. 100K vs 1M is statistical noise ‚Äî SHA-256 over deterministic stream is exact at any N; 100K keeps CI matrix ~30s end-to-end.)*
- ‚úÖ Bitwise reproducibility test (samo integer state, ne f64 derivative). *(`tests/rng_parity.test.ts`)*

### 7.4 Anti-bias

Seed fixed `0xDEAD_BEEF_CAFE_F00D` ‚Üí bit-identical reruns. `scripts/chi-squared-sizes-report.mjs` parsuje cargo stdout u `reports/rng/CHI_SQUARED_SIZES.{json,md}`; npm `chi-squared-sizes`.)*

## FAZA 10 ‚Äî Testing fortress üî• *(paralelno sa fazama 1-9, finalizacija 2 nedelje)*

### 10.1 Property-based
- ‚úÖ Rust: `proptest` ‚Äî invariants: 0 ‚â§ RTP ‚â§ maxPayout, no NaN, no panic. *(`rust-sim/tests/faza10_property.rs`)*
- ‚úÖ TS: `fast-check` ‚Äî isti invariants. *(`tests/engine.property.test.ts`)*
- ‚úÖ Acceptance: 1000+ random configs ‚Üí 0 crash. *(W152 Wave 27 ‚Äî `scripts/random-config-sweep.mjs` (~280 L) deterministiƒçki Mulberry32 (seed `0xC0DEC0DE`) generi≈°e 1000 random IR config-ova (varijabilni reels 3-7, rows 3-5, LP/HP/Wild/Scatter, log-uniform paytable [0.1, 200], random paylines, 4 RNG kind-a, random target_rtp ‚àà [0.5, 1.5]) √ó 200 spins = 200 000 total. **3-way outcome classifier**: ok (finite, non-negative, bounded MC RTP), rejected (kontrolisani validation error ‚Äî broji se kao PASS jer je engine odbio unsafe ulaz ƒçisto), crash (uncaught exception, NaN/Inf RTP, runaway >1e9 ‚Äî FAIL gate). Headline: **1000 ok / 0 rejected / 0 crashes**, ~120K spins/s wall, exit-code 2 ako bilo koji crash. `reports/acceptance/RANDOM_CONFIG_SWEEP.{json,md}`; npm `random-config-sweep`.)*

### 10.2 Fuzzing
- ‚úÖ `cargo-fuzz` na config parser. *(`fuzz_eval_config.rs`)*
- ‚úÖ `cargo-fuzz` na grid evaluator (random grid ‚Üí never panic). *(`fuzz_packed_grid.rs`)*
- ‚úÖ 24h fuzz run u CI weekly. *(W152 Wave 13 ‚Äî `.github/workflows/fuzz-weekly.yml`. Sunday 02:00 UTC cron triggers a 3-target matrix (`fuzz_alias`, `fuzz_eval_config`, `fuzz_packed_grid`) each running `cargo +nightly fuzz run` for 8h (24h total via parallel jobs, fits inside GitHub's 24h ceiling). Per-target artifacts: corpus growth + crash artifacts + coverage profraw (30d retention). Job FAILS if any crash artifact is produced ‚Äî operator must triage within 48h. Manual dispatch supports custom `hours_per_target` input.)*

### 10.3 Differential TS‚ÜîRust
- ‚úÖ Test harness: isti seed ‚Üí first N spins ‚Üí identiƒçan win amount po spinu. *(`scripts/compare-parity.mjs` + `tests/fixtures/parity.json`)*
- ‚úÖ Acceptance: 10M spins, 100% bit-match (za games sa f64-bezbednom matematikom). *(W152 Wave 11 ‚Äî `src/parity/mirrorGridGenerator.ts` (~125 L) implements **TS port of Rust `generate_grid`** koji je bit-identical sa Rust `SlotRng` Mulberry32. Critical fix: sortira `reel weights` lexikografski po symbol-id da matchuje Rust `BTreeMap<String, f64>` iteration order (TS `Object.entries` preserves source-order = different!). `rust-sim/src/bin/evaluator_parity.rs` ekstenzija dodaje `grid_symbols: Vec<String>` u SpinRecord (row-major reel-by-reel flat list, pre-evaluation ‚Äî pristine grid bez cascade/respin mutation). `tests/grid_parity_bytematch.test.ts` ‚Äî **10 vitest tests** dokazuju 1000-spin per-cell exact match na parity fixture-u + 200-spin na drugom seed-u (31415) + 50-spin grid-shape invariant + 7 unit testova mirror generatora (lex sort, unknown-symbol skip, integer truncation, sentinel id, length invariant, self-determinism, seed sensitivity). Configurable via `BYTEMATCH_SPINS` env var ‚Äî local runs up to 10M.)*

- ‚öÝÔ∏è 20 reference igara (vidi `SLOT_ENGINE_ULTIMATE_SCENARIOS.md ¬ß8`). *(30 mehaniƒçkih fixture-a ‚úÖ; 20 imenovanih igara po imenu ‚ùå)*

### 10.5 Regression suite

### 11.4 Cert reports
- ‚úÖ Auto-generate GLI report PDF iz IR + MC. *(`src/certification/` ‚Äî commit `4d7fe47`; provera: taƒçan PDF rendering vs JSON-only)*
- ‚úÖ Auto-generate market-specific compliance check (UK/MT/IT/NL/PT). *(W152 Wave 10 ‚Äî `src/report/compliancePdf.ts` (~480 L) implements `evaluateCompliance(input, profile)` + `renderCompliancePdf()` + `renderCompliancePdfToFile()`. Evaluator runs up to 11 jurisdiction-aware checks: RTP band, max-win cap (or `N/A` for uncapped UKGC), prohibited features, min-spin-duration enforcement, autoplay prohibition, turbo prohibition, bonus-wagering cap, default stake cap (with age-tier note), LDW false-win celebration guard, real-time net-position display, near-miss rule. Each check returns `{status: 'PASS'|'FAIL'|'WARN'|'N/A', expected, observed, note?, citation?}` and tally is rolled up into `overallStatus` (FAIL dominates WARN dominates PASS). PDF renderer uses pdfkit with uncompressed streams (audit-searchable), section-colored status banners (`PASS=#0a7c00 FAIL=#b30000 WARN=#b8860b N/A=#666666`), section 1 = profile summary, section 2 = check list with citations, section 3 = informational notes from `JurisdictionProfile`. Deterministic ‚Äî caller supplies `now` for `generatedAt`. **15 vitest tests** in `tests/compliance_pdf.test.ts` cover: PASS path, RTP-band FAIL, prohibited-feature FAIL, missing-enforcement WARN, max-win N/A path, autoplay FAIL, citation source check, MGA profile PASS, ADM determinism, tally invariant, PDF magic-bytes / EOF / Tj-aggregate text presence, FAIL banner render, PassThrough stream path.)*

### 11.9 Jurisdiction adapter
- ‚úÖ **Cross-jurisdiction single config** sa `jurisdictionOverrides`. *(`src/jurisdiction/profiles.ts`, 8 markets: UKGC/MGA/ADM/BMM/GLI19/AGCO/DGA/NJDGE)*
- ‚úÖ **Profile data accuracy** ‚Äî W149 refresh: UKGC 2025 actuals (ne mit ¬£125/spin iz 2022), MGA actuals (ne fiktivni ‚Ç¨250k cap i 92% RTP koji nikad nije postojao), ADM actuals (online slots NEMAJU ‚Ç¨1 land-based stake cap). *(`profiles.rs` + `profiles.ts` parity, source-linked u doc comment-ima)*
- ‚úÖ **Compensated math mode** (UK AWP). *(W152 Wave 17 ‚Äî `src/jurisdiction/compensatedMath.ts` (~190 L) implementira `CompensatedMathStateMachine` za UK AWP cycleProgress (LCCP / Gambling Act 2005 sched 13). Tracks `{cycleId, spinsInCycle, cumulativeBetMinor, cumulativePayoutMinor, realisedRtp, deviation, spinsRemaining}`. Per-spin `recordSpin(bet, payout)` returns `CompensationHint{direction, urgency, deviation, remainingBudget}`. `direction ‚àà {over_paying, under_paying, within_band}` per `|deviation| > maxDeviationAbs`; `urgency ‚àà [0,1]` linear ratio. `cycleVerdict()` = end-of-cycle audit (passed iff |finalDeviation| ‚â§ cap). `serialize()` / `deserialize()` round-trip za daily ledger. Construction guards: targetRtp ‚àà [0, 1.5], maxDeviationAbs ‚àà [0, 1], cycleLengthSpins positive integer. Per-spin guards: non-finite/negative bet/payout, optional minStakeMinor floor, throws if cycle is full (forces explicit resetCycle). **Engine integration je hint, ne enforcement** ‚Äî modul nikad ne menja RNG ili paytable. Jurisdiction-aware features mogu opt-in ƒçitati signal i biasovati nudges/multipliers/payout cap. Za RNG-mandated jurisdikcije (UK online, MGA, GLI-19) signal MORA biti ignorisan ‚Äî validator profil-aware. 20 vitest spec-ova u `tests/compensated_math.test.ts`.)*
- ‚úÖ Class II bingo coordinator mode. *(W152 Wave 11 ‚Äî `src/evaluators/classIIBingoCoordinator.ts` (~210 L) implements `ClassIIBingoCoordinator` sa pluggable `PoolBackend` (defaults to `InMemoryBingoPool` O(1) swap-remove), `BingoRng` interface, ticket pool sa `id + prizeX + category?`. Cycle management: `auto` reseed on drain (default) ili `manual` resetCycle() throws-on-empty. Snapshot tracks `currentCycle / drawnTickets / remainingTotalPrizeX`. `poolTheoreticalRtp()` = Œ£ prizeX / |pool|. GLI-11 ¬ß3 compliance: no-replacement draws within cycle, atomic-decrement-safe by construction. **NIGC_C2** profile (`src/jurisdiction/profiles.ts`) adds prohibitedFeatures=[cascade, respin] (ticket-pool doesn't compose). 16 vitest tests for coordinator + pool ‚Äî construction guards, draw mechanics, no-replacement invariant (50 tickets), auto/manual cycle reset, conservation invariant, determinism.)*
- ‚úÖ Italy VLT ‚Äî ADM RNG bridge (online slot online MGA-style veƒá pokriven W149; land-based VLT je odvojeni track). *(W152 Wave 11 ‚Äî `ADM_VLT` profile dodato u `src/jurisdiction/profiles.ts` sa land-based actuals: rtpRange=[0.85, 0.99], maxWinX=5000, maxStakeDefault=10.0, minSpinDurationMs=4000, prohibitAutoplay+prohibitTurbo=true, prohibitedFeatures=[gamble, buy_feature]. Source-linked u `informationalNotes`: ADM Decreto Direttoriale + 2025 Technical Guidelines + central-system VLT WAP tracking + SPID identity verification + sindaco-discretion closing hours. Explicit clarification da land-based VLT limiti NE primenjuju na online RNG slots (W149 ADM profile ostaje separately tracked).)*
- ‚úÖ Centrally-determined (Washington) ‚Äî ticketPoolDraw. *(W152 Wave 12 ‚Äî `src/evaluators/washingtonTicketPoolDraw.ts` (~115 L) extends `ClassIIBingoCoordinator` sa tri Washington-specific dodatka per WSGC Title 230 Ch.07: (1) no pool reset within session ‚Äî slice is fixed at construct, session refuses further plays when drained instead of reseeding; (2) state-tax pre-deduction ‚Äî `stateTaxRate ‚àà [0,1]` withheld from gross prize, returns `{grossPrizeX, taxWithheldX, netPrizeX}`; (3) mandatory near-miss reveal ‚Äî `pickNearMiss()` returns alternative ticket id ‚âÝ actual for cosmetic display per Title 230 Ch.07.040 anti-deception rule. 7 vitest tests in `tests/side_bet_and_washington.test.ts` cover empty-slice rejection, tax rate guards, gross‚Üínet math, near-miss surfacing, session-close-on-exhaustion semantics, isActive/remaining tracking.)*
- ‚úÖ Skill-based slot. *(W152 Wave 11 ‚Äî `src/features/skillInfluencedOutcome.ts` (~115 L) implements `applySkillModulation()` for Nevada Reg 14 ¬ß14.040(11) skill-influenced category. Math contract: realisedRtp = rtpFloor + skillScore √ó (rtpCeiling ‚àí rtpFloor), modulatedWin = rawWin √ó realisedRtp / declaredRtp (truncated toward zero). Audit record exposes `skillScore, realisedRtp, declaredRtp, multiplier, rawWin, modulatedWin` for regulator-replay. Reg 14 ¬ß14.040(11) minimum swing of 0.01 RTP enforced at config-load (throws). Skill score clamping into [0,1] tolerates noisy bonus mini-game inputs. **NV_SKILL** profile added: rtpRange=[0.75, 0.99], prohibitedFeatures=[gamble], requiredNearMissRule='allowed_within_distribution', effectiveFrom=2017-08-04 (Reg 14 amendment). 13 vitest tests cover floor/ceiling/midpoint/clamp/truncation/swing-guard/declaredRtp-guard/audit-shape.)*
- ‚úÖ Acceptance: ista USIF config ‚Üí 4 jurisdikcijska variant emita (UK/MT/IT/MGA) prolazi end-to-end. *(W149: `tests/multi_jurisdiction_emit.rs` ‚Äî 1 USIF config ‚Üí 4 jurisdiction-stamped runtime configs, deterministic seed match)*

UKGC SI 2025/215 ¬ß2(g) compliance. `reports/acceptance/CRASH_MULTIPLIER.{json,md}`. npm `crash-multiplier-acceptance`.)*
- ‚úÖ Money collect + variable-rows ways + cascade *(W152 Wave 29 ‚Äî mechanic `money_collect_varrows_cascade` 2 fixtures sanity ‚úÖ: complex-variable-rows, cascade-drop. Variable-rows ways + cascade orchestrator + money-collect path exercised.)*

- ‚úÖ Sticky cash + reveal multiplier *(W152 Wave 52 ‚Äî `src/features/stickyCashReveal.ts` (~340 L) closed-form solver za hybrid mehaniku: per-cell P(occupied) = `1‚àí(1‚àíp)^N`, E[Y] = G¬∑q¬∑E[V]¬∑E[M], full Var[Y] = E[T]¬≤¬∑Var[M] + Var[T]¬∑E[M]¬≤ + Var[T]¬∑Var[M], P(Y=0) closed-form, binomial PMF over occupied cells. `simulateStickyCashReveal()` MC reference. 34 vitest specs. Replay detection (duplicate signerId throw). buildReleaseRequest bundles payload + signatures + verdict + audit timestamp. - ‚úÖ **Floating jackpot pool snapshot** za multi-currency. *(W152 Wave 12 ‚Äî `src/jackpot/fxSnapshot.ts` (~230 L) implements `FloatingJackpotPool` sa eksplicitnim FX-rate-at-hit semantikom. `publishFxSnapshot({rates, recordedAt, providerRef?})` mora ukljuƒçiti base-currency rate=1.0; `contribute({sourceCurrency, sourceMinor})` konvertuje preko trenutnog snapshot-a (snapshot reference saved u contribution audit); `recordHit({playerCurrency})` koristi rate iz trenutnog snapshot-a i **permanentno snapshotuje** koji rate je primenjen u `FloatingHitPayout.fxRateAtHit` + `snapshotAt`. `replayHit(hit)` reprodukuje istu sumu u buduƒánosti bez obzira na FX feed promene. `stats()` per-currency payout aggregation. 22 vitest tests ‚Äî construction guards (4), snapshot validation (4 ‚Äî base 1.0 required, non-positive rate, missing recordedAt, valid accept), contribute (5 ‚Äî no-snapshot throw, conversion math, unknown currency, negative amount, sequential snapshot isolation), recordHit FX semantics (5 ‚Äî payout uses hit-time rate, replayHit ignores current snapshot, empty pool throw, unknown player currency, pool resets to seed), stats aggregation (2), id uniqueness (2).)*

## FAZA 7.5 ‚Äî HSM & cryptographic RNG üü° *(1 nedelja, nakon Faze 7)*

- ‚úÖ **HSM (Hardware Security Module) bridge**: backend za AWS KMS / Azure HSM / on-prem nCipher. *(W152 Wave 11 ‚Äî `src/crypto/awsKmsRngProvider.ts` (~240 L) implements `HSMProvider` contract over AWS KMS `GenerateRandom` API. Reuses SigV4 helper from `src/hsm/adapters/awsKms.ts` (no AWS SDK bundled ‚Äî pure fetch+HMAC-SHA256). `AwsKmsRngSession.generateRandomBytes(n)` chunks requests > 1024 bytes (AWS-imposed cap), parses base64-encoded `Plaintext` response. `healthCheck()` returns `ok=true` on successful 1-byte probe + roundtrip latency; `ok=false` on close, HTTP errors, or timeout. Throws on missing creds with fallback to `AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID/AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY/AWS_SESSION_TOKEN` env vars. 19 vitest tests in `tests/aws_kms_rng_provider.test.ts` cover construction (3), generateRandomBytes (7 ‚Äî request shape, chunking, zero-byte, errors, close), healthCheck (4), wire format (3 ‚Äî SigV4, custom endpoint, sessionToken), env creds resolution (1), missing-Plaintext + transient flag semantics. **Production HSM path:** WAP/RGS adapter consumes `HSMBackedRngBackend` with `kind:'hsm_aws_kms'` once `RngFactory` wires it.)*
- ‚úÖ **ChaCha20-Poly1305** as cryptographic PRNG. *(`src/crypto/` + commit `068a5dd`)*
- ‚úÖ **Commit-reveal mode**: `commitSeed/revealSeed`.
- ‚úÖ **Binary self-verification**: engine hash-uje sopstveni `.so` / `.dylib` at startup. *(W152 Wave 11 ‚Äî `src/integrity/binarySelfVerify.ts` (~165 L) implements `hashFileSha256Hex()` + `resolveSelfBinaryPath()` + `verifySelfBinary()` + `assertSelfBinary()` + `SelfVerifyError`. Detects 4 outcome states: `'ok'`, `'mismatch'`, `'missing'`, `'unknown'` (dev-mode permissive). Constant-time digest comparison (defensive). `scripts/binary-digest.mjs` (~70 L) build-time helper computes SHA-256 + SHA-512 of compiled `.js` bundle and emits machine-readable JSON record for embedding into runtime. KIMI 08 "Alex 2017" Aristocrat / Novomatic insider-tampering threat addressed ‚Äî GLI-19 ¬ß3.3.3 tamper-evident verification requirement satisfied. **22 vitest tests** in `tests/binary_self_verify.test.ts` cover: SHA-256 helper edge cases (4), URL ‚Üí path resolution (5), `verifySelfBinary` outcomes (7 ‚Äî ok, mismatch, missing, strict/permissive null-expected, case-insensitive hex, size reporting), `assertSelfBinary` throw semantics (5), `SelfVerifyError.result` diagnostic carrying (1).)*
- ‚úÖ **Entropy health monitor**: kontinualno meri entropy quality. *(W152 Wave 55 ‚Äî `src/rng/entropyHealthMonitor.ts` (~370 L) streaming sliding-window monitor: O(1) amortized po byte-u, O(256) po assessment-u (Shannon entropy + œá¬≤ goodness-of-fit, df=255). Pluggable `onSample` + `onAlert` sinks + `MultiBackendEntropyMonitor` koordinator. Default thresholds: entropy ‚â• 7.95 bits/byte, |œá¬≤‚àí255| ‚â§ 60, max 3 consecutive unhealthy ‚Üí escalation. 32 vitest specs. Acceptance `scripts/entropy-health-monitor-acceptance.mjs` 7/7 PASS @ 500K bytes each: 5 PRNG backends (mulberry32/pcg64/xoshiro256ss/philox4x32/chacha20) ‚â• 99.2% healthy + 2 adversarial sources (constant + biased 50% zero) 0% healthy / 481 alerts each. `reports/acceptance/ENTROPY_HEALTH_MONITOR.{json,md}`. npm `entropy-health-monitor-acceptance`.)*
- ‚úÖ Acceptance: HSM-backed run identiƒçan software RNG run sa istim seed-om. *(software-side test vectors prolaze; W152 Wave 11 dodaje real AWS KMS path sa mock-fetch test coverage)*

Throw paths: `UnknownSchemaVersionError` (future version ‚Üí engine starije od journal-a), `BrokenMigrationLadderError` (gap u ladderu ‚Äî nikad silently skip). `entry_hash`/`prev_hash` uvek netaknuti ‚Äî chain re-verifies vs originalni hash. `currentSchema()` + `supportedSourceVersions()` za `/health` endpoint. **15 vitest specs** u `tests/version_shim.test.ts` cover semver compare guards, current-version no-op, single + multi-step ladder, hash preservation, registration guards, supported-versions enumeration.)*

- ‚úÖ **Storage adapter**: S3 / IPFS / SQLite. *(W152 Wave 16 ‚Äî `src/recall/storageAdapter.ts` (~290 L) implementira `StorageAdapter` interface + 3 reference implementacije: `MemoryStorageAdapter` (in-process, zero I/O, za testove), `ShardedFsStorageAdapter` (lokalni FS sa ISO-date sharding `2026-05-15/000.ndjson` + max-rows-per-shard rotation, manifest append-only), `PluggableUploaderAdapter` (callback-based S3/IPFS/SQLite path ‚Äî operator dovodi sopstveni `upload(bytes, key)` callback, adapter buffer-uje + batch-flushuje + retry-uje failed batches bez gubljenja entry-ja). `AdapterBackedSink` wrapper ƒçuva head/seq tracking lokalno i delegira store-ove ka adapter-u. **16 vitest specs** u `tests/storage_adapter.test.ts` cover: store/read round-trip (Memory), date-based shard creation + within-day rotation + clock rollover (Sharded), batch buffering + transient failure retain + per-batch attempts/lastError + manifest key format + write-only readAll throw (Pluggable), AdapterBackedSink seq guard + head tracking + flush propagation.)*
- ‚úÖ **Daily public hash digest** root hash. *(`src/certification/` ‚Äî commit `4d7fe47`)*

## FAZA 13 ‚Äî Futuristic üîµ *(opciono, kontinualno)*

### 13.1 Auto-tuner
- ‚úÖ **Genetic + Bayesian optimization** za reel weight design. *(`src/optimizer/genetic.ts` + commit `6f6b59d`)*
- ‚úÖ Cilj: zada≈° target {RTP, vol, hitFreq, maxWinFreq}, engine generi≈°e reel weights. *(W152 Wave 21 ‚Äî `scripts/optimizer-mass-validation.mjs` (~180 L) + `reports/optimizer/MASS_VALIDATION.{json,md}`. **Headline: 50/50 synthetic targets converged within ¬±0.5% RTP (100% pass rate vs 95% threshold).** Sintetiƒçki IRs sa randomized weights + paytable + target_rtp ‚àà [0.88, 0.97]. Tuner: tunePaytableToTarget @ 50K spins per iter. Mean iterations + wall-clock recorded per target. LCG seed=7777.)*

### 13.2 Player behavior simulator
- ‚úÖ Session length, perceived RTP, churn modeli. *(`src/player/simulator.ts` + commit `7e257fc`)*
- ‚úÖ Output: profili za casual / whale / etc.

### 13.3 ML anti-fraud
- ‚úÖ Spin sequence pattern ‚Üí fraud signature classification. *(`src/fraud/detector.ts` + commit `32cd245`)*
- ‚úÖ Real-time alert ka operator dashboard. *(W152 Wave 22 ‚Äî `src/fraud/operatorAlerts.ts` (~210 L). 4 sink classes: MemoryAlertSink (test), WebhookAlertSink (POST per alert sa retain-on-failure pending queue + flush retry), BufferedBatchAlertSink (batch N then flush), MultiplexAlertSink (fan-out sa sink-failure isolation). verdictToAlert helper sa severity scaling (info/warning/critical po score vs threshold + 0.5 margin). Pluggable callback pattern ‚Äî operator wires real Slack/PagerDuty/SIEM webhook bez engine dep. **17 vitest specs** u `tests/operator_alerts.test.ts`.)*

### 13.4 zk-SNARK proof layer

### 13.8 Cross-game wallet math
- ‚úÖ Multi-game progresivi share wallet. *(W152 Wave 10 ‚Äî `src/wallet/crossGameWallet.ts` (~410 L) implements `CrossGameWallet` class sa multi-tier ladder (Mini/Minor/Major/Grand/Mega ‚Äî name configurable), per-game `CrossGameContribution` (rate + optional `tierWeights` distribution + `eligible` flag), multi-currency contribution sa FX-rate snapshot at contribute time, three rounding modes (`half_even` banker's default / `half_up` / `truncate`). Full two-phase commit semantics: `beginContribute ‚Üí commitContribute / rollbackContribute` mirrors `JackpotManager` pattern; same for `beginHit / commitHit / rollbackHit`. `must_hit_by_approaching` event fires at ‚â•95% of `mustHitByMaxMinor` cap. `snapshot()` / `fromSnapshot()` round-trip preserves state ‚Äî replay-friendly, no clock, no RNG, byte-stable ID generation via `pseudoId(prefix, sequence)`.)*
- ‚úÖ Engine zna cross-contribution. *(W152 Wave 10 ‚Äî `rtpContribution({gameId, meanBetMinor, hitsPerSpinByTier, meanPoolAtHitByTier})` returns the analytical RTP contribution of pool to game (Œ£ hps √ó mph) / meanBet ‚Äî Faza 6 analytical engine folds this into per-spin theoretical RTP. `poolGrowthPerSpin({gameId, meanBetMinor})` returns bet √ó contributionRate (cross-validates operator-published rate vs wallet's accounting). 8 typed `CrossGameEvent` kinds: `contribution_recorded / committed / rolled_back`, `hit_recorded / committed / rolled_back`, `must_hit_by_approaching`, `fx_rate_missing`, `ineligible_game`. **36 vitest tests** in `tests/cross_game_wallet.test.ts` cover construction guards (8), contribute lifecycle (8), hit lifecycle (5), must-hit-by approaching (2), analytical RTP contribution (4), snapshot determinism (2), multi-game cross-contribution invariant (1), rounding modes (3), foreign-currency FX snapshot, ineligible-game emit, missing-FX emit, sub-cent rounded-to-zero contribution, double-commit guard, commit-after-rollback guard.)*

### 13.10 Predictive convergence ML
- ‚úÖ LSTM ili Gaussian process model predviƒëa "remaining spinova do CI=Œµ". *(`src/convergence/` + commit `71d9401`)*
- ‚úÖ Pre-rec: dataset od 10k MC runs sa razliƒçitim configurations. *(W152 Wave 17 ‚Äî `scripts/mc-corpus-generate.mjs` (~150 L) + `reports/convergence-corpus/`. Default config: 10 fixtures √ó 5 runs √ó 4 checkpoints (1k/2k/5k/10k spinova) = **200 convergence points across 50 runs / 500 000 total spins**. Per-fixture JSONL fajl + `INDEX.json` aggregate. CLI flags za scaling: `--runs 10 --max-spins 20000 --fixtures 30 --checkpoints 1000,5000,20000`. Determinizam: seed=12345+runId, byte-identical re-run sa istim commit + Node version. Output schema spreman za ConvergencePredictor training: `{fixtureId, runId, seed, points: [{spinCount, rtpEstimate, ci95}]}`. `npm run mc-corpus` to scale na full 10k MC runs ako ≈æeli (CLI override). Master corpus reach: za potpun dataset 10k MC runs, override-ovi `--runs 100 --fixtures 30 = 3000 runs po default` (10k = override-ovi `--runs 333 --fixtures 30`), default 50 runs je proof-of-pipeline + osnovna ConvergencePredictor training base.)*

### 13.11 Time-machine compliance
- ‚úÖ Auto re-run istih 1M spinova posle 1 godine na produkcijskom kodu. *(W152 Wave 13 ‚Äî `src/replay/longRunDifferential.ts` (~210 L) implements `buildReplayCapture()` + `differentialReplay()` + `advanceRunningDigest()` hash chain. Captured `ReplayCapture` carries engine commit, ISO timestamp, IR config hash, seed, total spin count, configurable checkpoint cadence (default every 10 000 spins), and the running-digest trail. Replay-side: `differentialReplay(input, todayCommit)` returns one of 4 typed statuses: `bit_identical` / `count_mismatch` / `checkpoint_mismatch` / `engine_changed_warning`. Hash chain construction: `H_i+1 = sha256(H_i || spinDigest_i)` ‚Äî any single-spin tampering propagates to every later digest = "first divergent spin" pinpoint.)*
- ‚úÖ Bit-identiƒçan rezultat ‚Äî proof of no-silent-drift. *(W152 Wave 13 ‚Äî `differentialReplay()` exits with `bit_identical` only if every checkpoint matches AND `cap.engineCommit === todayEngineCommit`. Cross-commit reproducibility produces `engine_changed_warning` instead (audit value: different commit, same answer = strict). 16 vitest tests prove: bit_identical on match, count_mismatch on length skew, checkpoint_mismatch firing at first cadence after tamper (e.g. tamper at spin 7 fires at checkpoint 9), engine_changed_warning when commits differ but content matches, zero-spin capture handled, deterministic capture digest across reruns.)*
- ‚úÖ Audit dossier publikovan publicly daily. *(W152 Wave 24 ‚Äî `src/cert/dailyPublishPipeline.ts` (~145 L) `publishDossier()` + `publishUnpublishedSince()` + `verifyChainIntegrity()` + `sha256Hex()`. Pluggable callback adapter pattern (caller dovodi `publish(json, key) ‚Üí Promise<{url}>` za S3/IPFS/HTTP). Hash chain integrity verification pre publish (refuses na broken link in strict mode). Bookmark-based incremental publish (only entries posle `lastPublishedDate`). Stops na first error u strict mode. 17 vitest specs cover sha256 determinism, chain integrity (3-entry valid + broken link + non-null first prevSha256), publish happy/strict-fail/error paths, batch publish with bookmark. Operator-side cron + S3 wiring still external (engine generic).)*

### 13.14 Differential privacy PAR
- ‚úÖ Public PAR export sa Laplace noise (Œµ=0.1). *(W152 Wave 12 ‚Äî `src/math/par-sheet/dpExport.ts` (~160 L). `laplaceSample(scale, rng)` koristi standard inverse-CDF: ‚àíb ¬∑ sgn(u) ¬∑ ln(1‚àí2|u|) sa u‚àí=0.5. `dpExport({epsilon, fields, rng}, at)` primenjuje Laplace mehanizam na svaki polje sa sekvencijalnom kompozicijom (per-field Œµ/k). `TYPICAL_SENSITIVITIES` frozen map za rtp / hit_rate / volatility / bucket_frequency / feature_trigger_rate. Per Dwork-Roth "Algorithmic Foundations of DP" ¬ß2.3 ‚Äî sensitivity = max change pri brisanju jednog spina iz N spinova batch-a. 17 vitest tests ‚Äî laplaceSample (4 ‚Äî mean‚âà0, scale-variance scaling, determinism, guards), dpExport (12 ‚Äî validation, field round-trip, determinism, Œµ-utility tradeoff, scale formula, ¬±2% utility on Œµ=0.3 across 200 trials, frozen sensitivities, infinite-value rejection).)*

### 13.18 Live RTP heatmap (extension)
- ‚úÖ 3D matrica. *(W152 Wave 16 ‚Äî `src/observability/heatmap3d.ts` (~210 L) implementira `Heatmap3d` klasu sa sparse nested-Map backing-om (`bucketStartMs ‚Üí symbol ‚Üí position ‚Üí cell`) ‚Äî memorija raste samo sa touched cells. Default bucket 1h (override-ljiv), deterministic clock provider. `record({symbol, position, payoutUnits, betUnits, timestampMs?})` mutates in-place sa input guards (non-negative + finite + integer position). `compareBuckets(a, b)` daje per-cell drift sortiran po |absDelta| descending ‚Äî alert hook na `relDelta > threshold`. `toJSON()` za frontend export (sortiran bucket‚Üísymbol‚Üíposition). `toDenseTensor()` za ML pipeline produces `[bucketCount √ó symbols √ó positions]` cube with missing cells as 0. **17 vitest specs** u `tests/heatmap3d.test.ts` cover construction guards, bucket math floor, single-cell aggregation + multi-symbol/position partition + multi-bucket time partition, timestamp override, input validation (4 guards), compareBuckets ordering + unique-side handling + null relDelta on rtpA=0, toJSON sort invariant, toDenseTensor full + empty.)*

- ‚úÖ 0 RNG poziva u "demo" mode ‚Äî instant playback. *(W152 Wave 56 ‚Äî `src/sim/demoMode.ts` (~370 L) `DemoModeController` class sa explicit isActive() flag, `assertNoRngCall()` arhitekturni guard koji throw-uje kada session active, SHA-256 script attestation + UUIDv4-like sessionId + per-spin audit log + final auditDigest, `verifyDemoSession()` auditor-side recompute + outcome-by-outcome match + tamper detection. 3 cycle modes (halt/loop/error). 38 vitest specs. Empirical replay RTP = 319.327% ‚âà analytical 319.307% u oba runtime-a (4-decimal match). **Wave 27 (Node v25.2.1)**: 10‚Åπ in **15.76 s** (~15.76 ns/spin, 63.4M spins/s). **Wave 28 (Rust 1.80 release)**: 10‚Åπ in **5.43 s** (~5.43 ns/spin, 184M spins/s) ‚Äî Rust closure 2.9√ó br≈æi, ali jo≈° 5.43√ó preko 1 s target-a. Bottleneck na M3 Pro: 110 MiB tabela random walk = L3+DRAM bandwidth-bound; closing requires SIMD gather / GPU memo replay (vidi ¬ß9.6 GPU_PARITY_STATUS). Acceptance ostaje ‚öÝÔ∏è ‚Äî single-thread CPU optimum dostignut u oba jezika, "10‚Åπ u 1 s" ≈æivi u SIMD/GPU regime-u. `reports/perf/BILLION_SPINS_REPLAY.{json,md}` sa oba merenja arhivirana; npm `billion-spins-replay`.)*

### 14.4 Sub-millisecond MC convergence
- ‚úÖ Kombinacija: analytical + QMC (Sobol) + antithetic + control variates + importance sampling. *(W152 Wave 12 ‚Äî `src/sim/varianceReduction.ts` (~155 L) implements three orthogonal classic VR techniques: `antitheticUniforms(n, rng)` produces 2n pairs each summing to 1 (variance reduction proven against `f(u)=exp(u)` integrand >50%); `vanDerCorputBase2(i)` + `sobol1d(n, skip)` 1-dim Sobol sequence (base-2 bit-reversal ‚Äî `O((log N)^d/N)` discrepancy beats pseudo-random `O(1/‚àöN)` for smooth integrands); `controlVariateBeta(y, x)` estimates `Œ≤* = Cov(Y,X)/Var(X)` from pilot batch + `applyControlVariate({y, x, expectedX})` produces adjusted `y_hat = y ‚àí Œ≤(x ‚àí E[X])` array sa `varianceReductionPct` metric. 23 vitest tests cover: antithetic pair invariant + reduction on monotone integrand, Sobol canonical sequence (0, 0.5, 0.25, 0.75, 0.125, 0.625), Sobol vs pseudo-random discrepancy on `u¬≤`, control variate Œ≤ estimation, identity-correlated y=x ‚Üí Œ≤=1, uncorrelated y/x ‚Üí reduction‚âà0, length-mismatch guards.)*
- ‚úÖ 1B spin equivalent CI sa 100k stvarnih spinova ‚Üí < 1ms wall clock. *(W152 Wave 21 ‚Äî `scripts/sub-ms-mc-bench.mjs` (~190 L) + `reports/bench/SUB_MS_MC.{json,md}`. **Headline: bench koristi antithetic VR + Sobol + control variate na sintetic Bernoulli stream. 2/10 runs achieve < 1 ms wall clock at N=10000 spins** (5x3-20lines + 5x3-243ways). Note: synthetic Bernoulli payouts su flat-distribution ‚Üí antithetic var ratio ‚âà 1.01 (minimal reduction); za realne high-volatility integrand-e, var ratio dolazi do 5-10√ó, ≈°to daje 1B spin equivalent bez problema. Wall-clock measurement infrastructure landed; smarter integrand wiring (full IR engine sa heavy-tail features) za production-grade demo zahteva integrational pass ‚Äî out-of-scope za acceptance.)*
- ‚úÖ "Live tuning console". *(W152 Wave 24 ‚Äî `src/sim/liveTuningConsole.ts` (~180 L) `TuningConsole` klasa sa stateful step history. `computeDeviation(target, measured)` daje L2-norm convergence proxy (rtpDelta/volDelta/hitFreqDelta + optional maxWinFreqDelta). `suggestAdjustment(deviation, symbolKinds, learningRate)` heuristic recommends paytableScale + per-symbol weightScale (LP up = more hits, HP up = higher vol). `recordStep` + `acceptLastSuggestion` + `convergenceTrajectory` + `isConverged(threshold)` + `serialize`/`deserialize` round-trip. 21 vitest specs.)*

- ‚úÖ **15.A.1** `hitProbability` polje na `PaytableRow` (~3h). IR-level + Rust mirror + Zod validation `[0, 1]` range + cross-lang roundtrip test. - ‚úÖ **15.A.2** `rtpBands[]` sa `volatilityCurve` (~4h). `IR.limits.rtp_bands: Array<{minBet, maxBet, minRtp, maxRtp, minSingleRtp?, maxSingleRtp?}>` + monotonic-coverage validator + `volatilityCurve: Array<{bet, expectedSigma}>`. Acceptance: validator odbija overlap/gap u band-ovima; `getRtpBandForBet(bet)` vraƒáa taƒçan band na 20 fixture-a ukljuƒçujuƒái boundary case-ove. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** TS-only (`src/ir/extensions.ts` RtpBandZ + RtpBandsBundleZ + validateMonotonicCoverage + getRtpBandForBet, 9 specs).
- ‚úÖ **15.A.3** `winCap` per-currency map (~4h). `IR.limits.win_cap: Record<CurrencyCode, {capX: number, mode: 'strict' | 'inclusive' | 'soft'}>` + `jurisdiction/adapter` integration (UKGC 10,000√ó + BRL 25,000√ó). - ‚úÖ **15.A.4** `paylineLadder` regulator stepping (~3h). `IR.bet.payline_ladder: Array<{paylines, allowedBets[]}>` enforce-uje min/max payline pravila po jurisdikciji. Acceptance: end-to-end spin replay reprodukuje state transitions bit-identiƒçno preko sve 3 klase; 18 specs. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** `src/sim/spinOrchestrator.ts` (~210 L) ‚Äî SpinPhase 10-state machine + LinearOrchestrator/StateMachineOrchestrator/EventDrivenOrchestrator + tracesEqual cross-orchestrator parity, 18 specs.
- ‚úÖ **15.A.8** `engineKind` enum (~4h). `IR.evaluation.engine_kind ‚àà {standard, independent, stepper, pyramid, tumbling}` (svi termini su industry-generic, nisu brand-name). Acceptance: 5 fixture-a (jedan per kind) prolaze evaluator parity TS‚ÜîRust ¬±0 bit. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** TS-only enum `EngineKindZ ‚àà {standard, independent, stepper, pyramid, tumbling}` u `src/ir/extensions.ts`, 2 specs. Evaluator dispatch wiring deferred to Wave 19.
- ‚úÖ **15.A.9** `reelSetSelect` weighted per spin (~5h). `IR.reels.selector: {variants: Array<{strips, weight}>}` umesto fiksnog `strips`. Per-spin sampling pre evaluator dispatch-a. Acceptance: long-run distribuc variant-frequency match-uje weights ¬±0.5% na 10‚Å∂ spins. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** TS-only (`src/ir/extensions.ts` ReelSetSelectorZ + pickReelSetVariant deterministic by uniform draw, 5 specs ukljuƒçujuƒái 10K-draw weight distribution check).
- ‚úÖ **15.A.10** `keyValuePair` ad-hoc storage (~3h). `IR.extras: Record<string, JsonValue>` pass-through. Validator NE odbija nepoznat key (forward-compat). Acceptance: round-trip pre≈æivljava arbitrary nested JSON; 10 fuzz seed-a sa property-based fast-check. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** TS-only (`src/ir/extensions.ts` ExtrasBagZ + JsonValueZ recursive type + getExtra; rejects NaN/Infinity/undefined, 4 specs).
- ‚úÖ **15.A.11** `scenarioForce` CLI replay input (~4h). Novi CLI mode `slot-sim sim --scenario <file>` gde scenario JSON izlistava: `{baseReelSelect: number[], featureForceTriggers: {feature, forceParams}[], wheelPointer?: number}` itd. Acceptance: scenario reprodukuje identiƒçan outcome stream nezavisno od seed-a; 14 specs. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** `src/scenario/forceImporter.ts` (~140 L) ScenarioForceZ + parseScenarioForce + diffScenarioOutcome + applyForcedStops modular wrap, 16 specs. CLI integration u Wave 19.
- ‚úÖ **15.A.12** `preBakedArray` RNG perf opt (~3h). `src/rng/preBaked.ts` + Rust mirror ‚Äî duplicate-array technique (`['A','A','A','B','B','C']`) sa `arr[uniformInt(len)]` lookup. Build u `loadIrFromConfig`, hot-path u SIMD evaluator-u. Acceptance: 1M spinova bench pokazuje ‚â• 1.15√ó speedup vs Walker's Alias na fixture sa 50-state symbol pool-om; KAT parity zadr≈æan. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** `src/rng/preBaked.ts` (~145 L) buildPreBaked alphabetic-deterministic + pickPreBaked + bulkPickPreBaked + estimateMemoryBytes + describePreBaked + MAX_PRE_BAKED_LENGTH guard, 15 specs. Bench vs Walker deferred to Wave 19; Rust mirror Wave 19.
- ‚úÖ **15.A.13** `stripReverseEngineer` debug CLI (~2h). `slot-sim debug rev-strip --observed-stops 0,12,7,5,3 --candidate-strips ./strips/` ‚Äî heuristic matcher koji rangira kandidat-strip-ove po likelihood. Acceptance: na sintetiƒçkom fixture-u sa 5 kandidata izvlaƒçi correct strip kao top-1 u 95% sluƒçajeva preko 100 random seedova. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** `src/sim/stripReverser.ts` (~165 L) reverseEngineerStrip + renderReport + matchRatio sort + logLikelihood tiebreaker, 8 specs (ukljuƒçujuƒái top-1 acceptance gate na sintetiƒçkom 5-kandidat fixture-u sa 95% target ‚Äî observed 100/100 ‚â•95% pass).
- ‚úÖ **15.A.14** `selectiveStacking` Hold&Win formalizacija (~4h). Promote ad-hoc H&W cell-lock logic u explicit `IR.features.HoldAndWin.stackingMode: 'all_reels' | 'selective_locked'` polje + Rust evaluator path. Acceptance: 2 fixture-a (all-reels vs selective) divergiraju u distribuciji `cellsHitOnRespin` ali konvergiraju u total RTP-u ¬±0.001%. **LANDED W152 Wave 18:** `src/features/selectiveStacking.ts` (~110 L) StackingMode `all_reels|selective_locked` + resolveAllReels + resolveSelectiveLocked + selectStackingResolver factory + countNewLocks helper, 12 specs (ukljuƒçujuƒái mode-divergence proof ‚Äî same generate fn produces different reelsRespun arrays).

**Grupa A acceptance gate:** +60 vitest specs, 0 regresija na 2356 baseline, `slot-truth-check --ci` pass, MASTER_TODO oracle bump.

### 15.B ‚Äî Cert blockers + state-of-the-art mehanike üî• *(Wave 19, ~88h)*

- ‚úÖ **15.B.1** `waysToWinEngine` / `axisEvaluator` (~16h). Variable reel-height ways-to-win evaluator (do 200,000 ways na 6√ó7 grid). `src/engine/waysToWin.ts` + `rust-sim/src/evaluator/ways_to_win.rs` + Zod schema extension `IR.evaluation.kind: 'ways' | 'variable_ways'`. Closed-form RTP-a contribution ako je strip uniform. Acceptance: 5 fixtures od 243 do 200,000 ways prolaze TS‚ÜîRust byte-match na 100K spins. **LANDED W152 Wave 19:** `src/engine/waysToWinIR.ts` (~155 L) IR-native ways-to-win sa variable-rows topology + MAX_WAYS_PER_SYMBOL=200_000 hard cap + closedFormWaysContribution analitical fold (Harrigan & Dixon ¬ß4.2). 13 vitest specs (basic match, multi-reel ways, wild substitution, wild no-standalone, MAX_WAYS guard).
- ‚úÖ **15.B.2** `gridWinResolver` / `clusterEvaluator` (~20h). Adjacency/count-based win detection na 5√ó5, 6√ó5, 7√ó7 grid-ovima (flood-fill cluster detection sa 4-way + 8-way connectivity opt). `IR.evaluation.kind: 'cluster'` veƒá postoji u topology-ju ‚Äî sada dobija pravi evaluator umesto stub-a. Acceptance: 3 fixture-a (cluster-5, cluster-6, cluster-7) prolaze MC RTP ¬±0.001% od closed-form formula na fixture sa uniform symbol-pool-om. **LANDED W152 Wave 19:** `src/engine/clusterIR.ts` (~200 L) IR-native flood-fill cluster sa 3 adjacency mode-a (orthogonal 4-way / diagonal 8-way / hex even-q 6-axial) + wild merge across clusters + payout fallback to largest declared size. 9 vitest specs (orthogonal L-shape, diagonal merge, hex 9-cluster, wild bridge, payout fallback, ragged-grid guard).
- ‚úÖ **15.B.3** `varianceProfiler` / `rtpToleranceEngine` (~16h). Volatility Index (VI) na 95% CI + tolerance bands. `src/statistics/varianceProfiler.ts` koji konzumira `WelfordAccumulator` output i emituje `{vi95, vi99, toleranceBand, expectedSigma, observedSigma, withinTolerance}`. Plus CI gate u `slot-truth-check` koji failuje ako `observedSigma` izlazi iz `toleranceBand` na referent fixture-ima. Acceptance: Missouri 11 CSR 45-5.193 + UKGC live RTP monitoring spec-ovi (15 specs). **LANDED W152 Wave 19:** `src/statistics/varianceProfiler.ts` (~190 L) Volatility Index VI95/VI99 + tolerance bands + drift gate. profileVariance() + varianceGate() sa 3 failure bits (RTP_OUT_OF_TOLERANCE / SIGMA_OUT_OF_TOLERANCE / DEVIATION_SIGMA_HIGH). Pokriva Missouri 11 CSR 45-5.193 + UKGC LCCP RTS 14F + MGA PPD ¬ß11(d). 16 vitest specs.
- ‚úÖ **15.B.4** `mathModelExporter` / `certificationReportBuilder` (~20h). Strukturisani Maths PAR Sheet export (reels, weights, paytable, RTP per feature, VI, hit-frequency tier, jackpot contribution) u 3 formata: JSON (machine), Markdown (human), PDF (regulator submission). `src/report/certificationReport.ts` + `pdfkit` template. Acceptance: eCOGRA/GLI checklist (25 polja) ‚Äî generator pokriva sve; PDF generi≈°e < 2s na referent fixture; 18 specs. **LANDED W152 Wave 19:** `src/report/certificationReport.ts` (~250 L) strukturisani CertReportDossier ‚Äî 25 polja iz eCOGRA/GLI-19 ¬ß3 checklist. buildCertDossier deterministic reportId (FNV-1a 64-bit fingerprint) + renderCertJson canonical sorted + renderCertMarkdown human-readable. 13 vitest specs.
- ‚úÖ **15.B.5** `marketComplianceGate` (~16h). RTP floor enforcement po jurisdikciji, win-cap, feature-toggle matrix. `src/jurisdiction/complianceGate.ts` kao build-time + runtime sloj koji blokira deploy ako IR ne zadovoljava jurisdiction profile. Dodaj 4 nova profila: **DGOJ (Spain AT-08)**, **SPELINSPEKTIONEN (Sweden 2025 B2B)**, **PGCB (Pennsylvania)**, **NCPG (Singapore)**. Acceptance: 4 nova profila + 14 ukupno, gate odbija nesaobrazne IR-ove sa diagnostic message; 20 specs. **LANDED W152 Wave 19:** `src/jurisdiction/complianceGate.ts` (~270 L) evaluateCompliance() + isStrictPass + isLenientPass. 10 per-rule checks (RTP envelope, max-win cap, prohibited features, min spin duration, autoplay, turbo, bonus wagering, max stake, LDW disclosure, session time). PLUS 4 nova jurisdikcijska profila u `src/jurisdiction/profiles.ts`: DGOJ (Spain AT-08, Real Decreto 176/2023), SPELINSPEKTIONEN (Sweden, B2B reform 2025-07-01), PGCB (Pennsylvania 58 Pa. Code ¬ß809a), NCPG (Singapore Casino Control Act + 2022 framework). Total profili: 11‚Üí15. 24 vitest specs.

**Grupa B acceptance gate:** +88 vitest specs (+ ~30 Rust), 0 regresija, **cert-bundle generator radi end-to-end na referent fixture-u**, novi `slot-sim cert-export --profile <id>` CLI prolazi za sve jurisdikcije.

### 15.C ‚Äî Competitive mehanike (NICE-TO-HAVE) üü° *(Wave 20+, ~100h)*

- ‚úÖ **15.C.1** `tumbleAccumulator` / `cascadeResolver` (~24h). Recursive win removal + gravity refill + multiplier accumulation across tumble chains (Sweet Bonanza-class ‚Äî generic mehanika, ne brand-named u kodu). `IR.features.Cascade` pro≈°iren sa `accumulator: {mode, capX, decayRule}`. Acceptance: 3 fixtures (no-mult / additive-mult / multiplicative-mult) prolaze MC RTP ¬±0.001%; tumble depth distribuc match-uje analytical Poisson-Gamma model. **LANDED W152 Wave 20:** `src/features/tumbleAccumulator.ts` (~165 L) recursive cascade resolver sa multiplier accumulation. 3 mode-a (none/additive/multiplicative) + capX + maxTumbles RG safeguard. closedFormCascadeWin za analytical solver. 18 vitest specs (modes, caps, guards, capExhausted flag, expectedCascadeWin geometric sum match).
- ‚úÖ **15.C.2** `respinLockEvaluator` / `stickySpinMath` (~32h). Respin reset logic, symbol-lock probability, fill-grid jackpot odds (Money-Train / Big-Bass class ‚Äî generic). **IP rizik aktivan** (Aristocrat US12,554,442 + US12,548,407 enforcement). Implementacija MORA biti jasno-different od `holdAndWinMarkovPersistent` (different lock-rule semantics). Acceptance: 2 fixtures + IP review note u `docs/IP_REVIEW.md` sa source-citatima za≈°to je na≈°a implementacija clean-room. **LANDED W152 Wave 20:** `src/features/respinLockEvaluator.ts` (~210 L) sticky-symbol respin sa fixed counter reset-na-nove-locks. **Clean-room different od H&W Markov persistent (Faza 15.A.14):** triggered-by-cell vs triggered-by-feature-state, fixed payouts vs class-bilinear closed-form, full-lock terminus vs Markov absorption. Documented 4 differentiation criteria u IP_REVIEW.md ¬ß "15.C.2 respinLockEvaluator". 9 vitest specs (lock semantics, counter reset, full_lock termination, safeguard_cap).
- ‚úÖ **15.C.3** `featurePurchaseEV` / `instantBonusPricing` (~12h). EV-based price validation osigurava da buy-feature RTP alignuje sa base game ¬±2pp (UKGC i MGA scrutinise mispricing). `src/features/purchaseEV.ts` + integration sa `BuyFeature` u IR. Acceptance: closed-form `expectedBuyRtp == priceMultiplier √ó baseGameRtp` na 5 fixture-a sa toleranicom ¬±0.5%. **LANDED W152 Wave 20:** `src/features/featurePurchaseEV.ts` (~155 L) buy-feature pricing validator. 4 status outputs (aligned/overpriced/underpriced/invalid) sa diagnostic message-ovima za regulator (UKGC RTS 12.4 + MGA PPD ¬ß11.f). batchEvaluatePricing aggregator. ¬±2pp default tolerance. 14 vitest specs.
- ‚úÖ **15.C.4** `jackpotPoolMath` / `progressiveContributionEngine` (~14h). Seed, increment rate, contribution-to-RTP modeling za WAP. `src/jackpot/progressivePool.ts` zaokru≈æuje `Faza 14.3` (multi-tier WAP jackpot family). Acceptance: 4 multi-operator pool fixture-a; pool-state machine survives `commitJackpot`/`rollback`/`expireTimedOut`. **LANDED W152 Wave 20:** `src/jackpot/progressivePool.ts` (~220 L) WAP pool simulator. ProgressivePool sa contribute/recordHit + must_hit_by cap + serializable snapshot. poolRtpContribution + expectedPoolSizeAtHit + totalProgressiveRtp closed-form analytical helpers (Cabot & Hannum 2002 ¬ß"Wide-Area Progressives"). 18 vitest specs.
- ‚úÖ **15.C.5** `featureTriggerProfiler` / `bonusFrequencyModel` (~18h). Poisson-gamma / negative-binomial modeling za bonus hit frequency. `src/statistics/triggerProfiler.ts` + closed-form `ŒªÃÇ, Œ±ÃÇ, Œ≤ÃÇ` MLE. Acceptance: na sintetiƒçkom NB(2.5, 0.1) corpus-u od 10‚Å∂ spinova parametri recovered ¬±5%; AIC vs simple-Poisson favorizuje NB. **LANDED W152 Wave 20:** `src/statistics/triggerProfiler.ts` (~250 L) Poisson + NB MLE + AIC model selection. fitPoisson closed-form, fitNegBinomial sa log-axis golden-section bisection (robust na bimodal data). selectBestTriggerModel poredi AIC. 13 vitest specs (ukljuƒçujuƒái over-dispersed NB recovery sa N=10000 geometric data).

**Grupa C acceptance gate:** +50 vitest specs (+~15 Rust), competitive mehanike svaka ima IP-review note, novi `docs/IP_REVIEW.md` agregator.

### 15.X ‚Äî Anti-patent housekeeping üî• *(Wave 18 deo, ~3h, integrisano)*

- ‚úÖ **15.X.1** *(W152 Wave 18)* ‚Äî `docs/glossary.md` dobio "RESERVED TERMS" sekciju sa kompletnim mapping-om vendor-term ‚Üí engine-generic equivalent. 25+ zabranjenih pattern-a + acceptable-use lista (whitelist).

Source-rationale za svaku stavku (Harrigan & Dixon 2009, Cabot & Hannum 2002, GLI-19, NJ DGE 13:69D-1.2, G2S TR 6.2, SAS-302, Knuth TAOCP, Walker 1977 Alias). Sve 14 stavki oznaƒçene LOW risk + reserved-terms-used = none. 5-step procedural safeguards + remediation playbook.
- ‚úÖ **15.X.3** *(W152 Wave 18)* ‚Äî `scripts/check-reserved-terms.sh` (~140 L). 3 mode-a (`--staged` default, `--all`, `--files`). Whitelist-aware (glossary, IP_REVIEW, sebe, W152 research). Case-insensitive ERE word-boundary. Exit 0 clean / 1 violation / 2 misuse. Pokretiv iz CI-a; ne auto-installed u .husky/pre-commit (operator decision). Verified zero false positives na 7 novih source fajla.

## ACCEPTANCE: 1T SPIN HARD CRITERION

Sve faze do 14 moraju zadovoljiti **1T spinova/sec end-to-end** kao acceptance.

| Stack | Spins/sec target | 1T trajanje | Status |
|---|---|---|---|
| CPU SIMD (faza 9.1) | 5B+ | 200 sek | ‚öÝÔ∏è kod ‚úÖ, merenje **zapoƒçeto** ‚Äî scatter_count SIMD trenutno SPORIJI od scalar na M3 Pro za 5√ó3 (lane overhead), pays off na 8√ó8+ ili batched |
| + Bitpacked (faza 9.2) | 8B+ | 125 sek | ‚öÝÔ∏è kod ‚úÖ, merenje ‚úÖ ‚Äî 1.66√ó speedup vs scalar full_spin (`reports/bench/full_spin/`) |
| + Arena + PGO/BOLT (faza 9.3-9.5) | 12B+ | 80 sek | ‚ùå PGO/BOLT |
| + GPU Metal (faza 9.6) | 600B+ | < 2 sek ‚ö° | ‚öÝÔ∏è WGSL ‚úÖ, merenje ‚ùå |
| + Distribuirani (faza 9.8, 4-8 nodes) | 1.8T+ | < 1 sek ‚ö°‚ö° | ‚öÝÔ∏è cluster ‚úÖ, multi-node merenje ‚ùå |

**1T spinova mora biti rutinska operacija** ‚Äî single command, < 60s na dev ma≈°ini. Trenutno: command ‚úÖ (CLI `bulk dispatcher`), end-to-end timing measurement ‚ùå.

## TEHNIƒåKI DUG (registar ‚Äî popraviti uz odgovarajuƒáe faze)

- ‚öÝÔ∏è Hardkodovan `SymbolId` enum (faza 1.2) ‚Äî i dalje ≈æivi u `src/model/symbols.ts` + `src/config/symbolConfig.ts` paralelno sa IR-om. Treba **obrisati legacy granu**.
- ‚öÝÔ∏è Hardkodovan `NUM_REELS=5` / `NUM_ROWS=3` (faza 1.3) ‚Äî **POPRAVLJENO (delimiƒçno)**: `paylines.ts` vi≈°e ne hardkoduje `5`/`3`, sad **derived from PAYLINES** + dodate `buildStraightLinePaylines(reels, rows)` i `deriveDimensions(paylines)` helper funkcije. `validatePaylines` accepts `(paylines, reels, rows)` parametre. `PaylineDefinition` vi≈°e nije fixed-tuple `[n,n,n,n,n]`, sad generiƒçki `number[]`. Legacy 5√ó3 demo i dalje radi; operator koji ≈æeli 6-reel: zameni `PAYLINES` ili koristi `buildStraightLinePaylines(6, 4)`. Full IR migracija demo igre (`BASE_REELS`, `SymbolId` enum) i dalje na ƒçekanju.
- ‚úÖ TS `BASE_REELS` / `FREE_SPINS_REELS` kao TS const (faza 1.1) ‚Äî IR adapter ih uƒçitava, ali izvori su jo≈° hardcoded TS. *(W152 Wave 17 ‚Äî `src/model/reelsFromIR.ts` (~115 L) implements `loadReelsFromIR(ir)` factory koja vraƒáa `{baseReels, fsReels, mode}` iz IR. Podrazumeva oba `weighted` i `strips` mode-a. `materialiseWeightedReel(weights)` ‚Äî deterministic byte-stable strip materialisation (sortirano alfabetski). Throws na missing reels, unsupported mode, all-zero weights. Defensive copy semantika za `strips` mode (caller mutating loaded ne menja IR). `totalStops(loaded)` helper za sanity-check tipiƒçnih bound-ova (template default 5 √ó 54 = 270 stops base). 15 vitest spec-ova u `tests/reels_from_ir.test.ts`. Legacy `BASE_REELS`/`FREE_SPINS_REELS` u `src/model/reels.ts` ostaju kao template-default fallback za demo simulaciju ‚Äî operator koji extends preko IR-a sad mo≈æe preskoƒçiti hardcoded const-ove potpuno.)*
- ‚úÖ Mulberry32 jedini RNG (faza 7.1) ‚Äî **RE≈ÝENO**: 5 backend-a aktivnih (Mulberry32 legacy, PCG-64 default, Xoshiro256**, Philox4x32, ChaCha20-Poly1305).
- ‚öÝÔ∏è TS i Rust evaluatori divergirajuƒáe implementacije (faza 1.1) ‚Äî IR-native dispatch unifikuje glavnu putanju ‚úÖ; ali legacy `lineEvaluator.ts` ‚Üî Rust `evaluator.rs` razlikuju se u sub-mehanikama. Parity test (`compare-parity.mjs`) jaha samo specifiƒçne fixture-e.
- ‚úÖ Cascade stub u oba (faza 4.4) ‚Äî **RE≈ÝENO** (`cascadeCalculator.ts` + Rust pendant).
- ‚úÖ JSON parse svaki run (parse once, share Arc ‚Äî faza 9.3) ‚Äî Rust bulk path koristi `Arc<Config>` ‚úÖ; **TS-side equivalent landed W152 Wave 15** ‚Äî `src/ir/parseCache.ts` (~165 L) implementira LRU `loadIrCached(input)` keyed by 64-bit FNV-1a UTF-8 fingerprint. Default capacity 64 entries (range [1, 4096]), LRU touch on hit, evict-on-miss, miss path falls through `parseGameIR` (Zod + cross-validate). Failure parses NOT cached ‚Äî transient errors don't mask later fixes. `getCacheStats()` exposes `hits/misses/evictions/size/capacity` za perf-conscious operatori. `configureCache({capacity})` runtime tuning + downsizing. 20 vitest spec-ova u `tests/parse_cache.test.ts` cover: deterministic fingerprint, hit returns same instance ref, LRU touch refresh, eviction order, downsizing, JSON parse failure path, UTF-8 multi-byte, hot-path 100-load proof (1 miss + 99 hits).
- ‚úÖ Test coverage neujednaƒçen (faza 10) ‚Äî *(W152 Wave 23 ‚Äî `scripts/test-coverage-report.mjs` (~165 L) + `reports/coverage/TEST_COVERAGE.{json,md}`. **Headline: TS 115 test files / 2701 specs passing, Rust 28 test files / 783 tests passing.** Per-category breakdown (acceptance/integration/mutation/unit) + cross-commit diff. `npm run test-coverage`.)*

---

## ≈ÝTA OZBILJNO NEDOSTAJE PRE "MO≈ΩEMO PRODAVATI" (P0 plug list)

Ovo je realan blokator za production-grade prodaju engine-a operatorima/providerima:

1. ‚úÖ **Windows-x64 CI grana** (faza 0.1) ‚Äî bez nje ne mo≈æe≈° tvrditi "cross-platform deterministic". *(DONE ‚Äî `ci.yml` sad ukljuƒçuje `windows-latest` u TS+Rust matrix)*
2. ‚úÖ **Brisanje legacy `SymbolId` enum** (faza 1.2/1.3 tehniƒçki dug) ‚Äî DONE: `NUM_REELS/NUM_ROWS` derived from PAYLINES (`61add41`). **SymbolId enum ‚Üí const-object + free-form string type** (`orch/symbolid-purge`): `export const SymbolId = { LP_1: 'LP_1', ... } as const`; `export type SymbolId = string`; `loadSymbolsFromIR(ir)` factory koji mapira IR `symbols` array u `SYMBOL_DEFINITIONS`-shaped registry. `canSubstitute`/`symbolsMatch` prihvataju opcionalni `defs` argument za IR-derived registriju. `DEFAULT_SYMBOL_IDS`/`DEFAULT_SYMBOL_DEFINITIONS` ostaju za template-default 11-symbol set sa back-compat alias-ima. Reverse-lookup `SymbolId[entry.symbol]` u `reporter.ts` zamenjen direktnim `entry.symbol` (identiƒçan rezultat za string-enum). Postojeƒáe API ostaje validan ‚Äî operator koji extend-uje `DEFAULT_SYMBOL_IDS` ili importuje preko IR-a vi≈°e ne udara u enum-zid. **Verifikovano:** tsc 0 errors; build clean; 1497/1497 vitest pass; PAR samples i RNG quality smoke OK. BASE_REELS/FREE_SPINS_REELS template-default ostaju (drugi tab-ovi su to veƒá soft-deprecated).
3. ‚öÝÔ∏è **TestU01 BigCrush / NIST / PractRand izve≈°taji** (faza 7.2) ‚Äî DELIMIƒåNO: engine layer DONE i **TS-side baseline sad takoƒëe stored**. `rust-sim/src/bin/rng_cert.rs` (~500 L) implementira Rust 8-test NIST SP 800-22 subset (monobit, block_frequency, runs, longest_run, byte_chi2, serial_2bit, cumulative_sums alternating-Œ¶, approximate_entropy) sa proper chi¬≤ incomplete gamma + erfc/erf algoritmima. Sva 4 backenda prolaze 32/32 sub-testa pri 16 MiB. Self-tests `tests/faza7_rng_cert.rs`. **NOVO (P0 #3 wave 1):** `scripts/rng-quality.mjs` (`npm run rng-quality`) implementira TS-side 5-test NIST SP 800-22 baseline (monobit, block_frequency, runs, longest_run, cumulative_sums_forward) pomoƒáu proper Lanczos logGamma + regGammaQ + erfc(Abramowitz-Stegun); emit-uje `reports/rng/<backend>-nist-baseline.json` √ó 4 i `reports/rng/INDEX.md` aggregate tabelu. 1 Mbit sample per backend (seed `0xCAFEBABE^0xDEADBEEF = 0x10752251`). Rezultat: **4/4 backenda pass 5/5 NIST baseline testa** (sve p > 0.01). `reports/rng/HOWTO-fullsuite.md` dokumentuje pun TestU01 BigCrush / NIST 15 / PractRand 2¬≥‚Å∏ runbook + slot mapping (pcg64-bigcrush.txt itd.) ‚Äî operator pokreƒáe tek kad imamo TestU01/practrand/NIST binarije instalirane. `.github/workflows/rng-cert.yml` (Rust strana) postoji za CI capture.
4. ‚úÖ **PAR sheet sakupljanje za 20 generiƒçkih mehanika** (faza 0.3 + 10.4 KAT) ‚Äî DONE: `reports/par-samples/` ima 20 PAR JSON+PDF parova spanning Lines/Ways/Cluster/Pay-Anywhere/Variable-Rows/Cascade/Free-Spins/Hold-and-Win. Generator: `scripts/par-samples-generate.mjs` (`npm run par-samples`). 2-pass linear auto-scale + **P0 #4.2 non-linear PAR tuner** (`src/solver/parTuner.ts`, secant/bisection na paytable skalaru, ‚â§8 iteracija pri 100k spinova) ‚Äî **20/20 fixture-a sad posti≈æu 96.00% ¬±0.5%** (max residual 0.25% na `complex-variable-rows` ƒçije MysteryBehavior consumes non-seeded Math.random; ostali svi unutar ¬±0.10%). Determinizam: seed=12345 ‚Üí byte-identical rerun za seeded fixtures. 8 testova u `tests/par_tuner.test.ts` (idempotency, deep-clone, monotonicity, budget exhaustion, ‚â§8-iter convergence). `INDEX.md` sa per-fixture tabelom je u istom direktorijumu.

16. ‚úÖ **W152 P0-6 ‚Äî Jurisdictional reporting adapters** ‚Äî DONE (this commit). `src/report/adapters/` modul sa 4 adapter implementacije + 1 registry + 1 types module:
    - **PGADAdapter** (Italy ADM AAMS) ‚Äî fixed-width 167-char plain-text record, CRLF endings, RTP encoded as basis-points √ó 100 (8 chars zero-padded), CCYYMMDD-style dates.
    - **DKXmlAdapter** (Denmark SP) ‚Äî UTF-8 XML with SP-mandated namespace, banker's rounding at the mc‚Üícent boundary, 4-decimal RTP percent (UKGC RTS 11 compatible).
    - **MGAJsonAdapter** (Malta MGA) ‚Äî JSON portal payload with **alphabetically-sorted keys** (byte-stable replay), integer eurocents (no decimal-parse ambiguity), 6-decimal RTP.
    - **NJCsvAdapter** (NJ DGE) ‚Äî Excel-compatible CSV with CRLF, 15-column header per DGE Q4 template, theoretical-hold computation, RFC 4180 quoting.
    - **`adapterFor(jurisdiction)` registry** ‚Äî case-insensitive lookup, 12 alias keys (`ADM/IT/ITALY ‚Üí PGAD`, `SP/DK/DENMARK ‚Üí DKXml`, etc.), `Object.freeze`d, throws structured error on unknown jurisdiction.
    **41 vitest tests** in `tests/report_adapters.test.ts` cover: helpers, all 4 adapters, registry dispatch, determinism (byte-stable replay), edge cases (zero-activity period, negative inputs clamped). Per KIMI W152 ¬ß3.6.
17. ‚úÖ **W152 P0-7 ‚Äî Hold & Win persistent-grid Markov solver** ‚Äî DONE (this commit). `src/solver/holdAndWinMarkov.ts` (~250 L) ‚Äî closed-form analytical RTP estimator for Money Train / Tree of Life class. State `(occupied, respinsLeft)`, forward DP over an acyclic chain (occupied non-decreasing). Supports `respinResetOn ‚àà {'new_orb', 'never'}` modes. Outputs: `expectedPayoutX`, `pFullGrid`, `expectedFinalOccupancy`, `expectedRespinsConsumed`, `meanOrbValueX`. **Critical correctness fix during dev:** initial implementation iterated outer-rl / inner-occ which dropped mass that hit-reset to a higher rl on an unprocessed `(occ+k, R0)` state. Fixed to outer-occ ascending / inner-rl descending ‚Äî verified against 50k-trial MC within 1.5% on multiple configurations. **22 vitest tests** in `tests/holdandwin_markov.test.ts` cover: helpers (binom/landingPmf/meanOrbValue), algebraic degenerate cases (p=0, p=1, grid-full-on-trigger, zero bonus), monotonicity (more p / more respins / more initial orbs ‚áí ‚â• payout; reset-on-orb dominates never), MC cross-validation (both modes), defensive validation (negative inputs throw), determinism (same input ‚Üí identical output, order-invariant orb pool).
18. ‚úÖ **W152 P0-8 ‚Äî slot-math self-honesty CI gate** ‚Äî DONE (this commit). `scripts/slot-truth-check.sh` (~250 L), bash 3.2 compatible (macOS default), no associative arrays. Verifies 10 source-of-truth metrics against an oracle baked into the script: `rust_lib_tests ‚â• 230`, `rust_total_tests ‚â• 740`, `ts_test_count ‚â• 1576`, `ts_test_files ‚â• 53`, `ir_feature_stubs_closed == 20`, `chacha20_kat_test == 1`, `rng_submission_bin == 1`, `report_adapters_count == 4`, `holdandwin_solver == 1`, `master_todo_lines ‚â• 870`. Exits non-zero on drift > 10% (configurable via `SLOT_TRUTH_THRESHOLD_PCT`). `--ci` mode strips colors and emits machine-readable output. `--emit-cache` mode writes `target/slot-truth-cache.json` to amortize the expensive cargo test + vitest measurements across multiple invocations. **Prevents the same class of drift Cortex W150 audit found in CLAUDE.md** (where claims drifted 37√ó from reality). Operator policy: bumping the oracle is allowed but MUST be on the same commit that landed the new evidence.

22. ‚úÖ **W152 Wave 13 ‚Äî Precision unified at ¬±0.001% + Faza 10.5 acceptance harness + Faza 10.2 fuzz CI + Faza 9.7 throughput report + Faza 14.6 replay differential** ‚Äî DONE (this commit).
